focus_tree = {
	id = Syria_2000
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			OR = {
				original_tag = SYR
				original_tag = FSA
				original_tag = NUS
			}
		}
	}
	default = no

	shared_focus = SYR_diplomatic_effort
	shared_focus = SYR_greater_syria
	shared_focus = SYR_military_reform

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 1300 y = 1700 }

	#Main succession branch
	focus = {
		id = SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad
		icon = national_unity_red

		x = 9
		y = 0

		cost = 10

		available = { always = no }

		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TT_DEATH_OF_HAFEZ
				has_country_flag = Syria_Hafez_dead
			}
		}

		completion_reward = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad" }

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
			}
		}
	}
	##Bushra's branch
	focus = {
		id = SYR_bushra_al_assad
		icon = Bushra_al_Assad

		x = 3
		y = 1

		cost = 5

		prerequisite = { focus = SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = SYR_bashar_al_assad
			focus = SYR_maher_al_assad
			focus = SYR_flowers_of_damascus_spring
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		available = {
			emerging_autocracy_are_in_power = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Syrian_rebels }
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_bushra_al_assad"
			hidden_effect = { kill_country_leader = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 15 }
			set_temp_variable = { col_one = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { col_two = 13 }
			set_temp_variable = { col_three = 18 }
			set_temp_variable = { col_four = 19 }
			change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Bushra al-Assad"
				picture = "Bushra_Al-Assad.dds"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					neutrality_oligarchism
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { max_leader = bushra_popularity }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < bashar_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = bashar_popularity }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < maher_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = maher_popularity }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { stability_loss = bushra_popularity }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_loss = max_leader }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_loss = 0.01 }
			add_stability = stability_loss
			set_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = bushra_popularity }
			multiply_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = 0.005 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = leader_popularity }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = leader_popularity }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			recalculate_party = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1.9
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { bushra_popularity > bashar_popularity }
						check_variable = { bushra_popularity > maher_popularity }
					}
					neutrality > 0.4
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }

				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			recalculate_party = yes
		}

					AND = {

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_deal_with_scraps
	icon = syria_resistance

	x = -9
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = SYR_greater_syria

	cost = 10

	prerequisite = { focus = SYR_lebanese_chaos }

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = LEB
				NOT = { country_exists = HEZ }
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = HEZ
				NOT = { country_exists = LEB }
			}
		}
	}

	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = LEB }
		NOT = { country_exists = HEZ }
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_deal_with_scraps"
		if = {
			limit = { LEB = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = LEB }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			annex_country = { target = LEB transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { HEZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			annex_country = { target = HEZ transfer_troops = yes }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = HEZ }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = LEB }
			LEB = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.52 hours = 6 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = HEZ }
			HEZ = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.52 hours = 6 } }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = LEB }
				annex_country = { target = LEB transfer_troops = yes }
				every_core_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = LEB }
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { country_exists = HEZ }
				annex_country = { target = HEZ transfer_troops = yes }
				every_core_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = HEZ }
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_assault_jordan
	icon = anti_monarchism2

	x = -7
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = SYR_greater_syria

	cost = 10

	prerequisite = { focus = SYR_lebanese_chaos }
	will_lead_to_war_with = JOR

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no
		country_exists = JOR
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JOR }
	}

	bypass = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = JOR }
			JOR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_assault_jordan"
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_SYR_ASSAULT_JORDAN
		set_temp_variable = { success_chance = JOR.party_popularity@nationalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { success_chance = 200 }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = success_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = success_chance }
		set_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = remaining_chance }
		multiply_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = 0.5 }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = civil_war_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = civil_war_chance }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = remaining_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = success_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.55 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = civil_war_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.57 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = remaining_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.58 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			211 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			210 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			212 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			annex_country = { target = JOR transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_REJECT
		effect_tooltip = {
			JOR = { declare_war_on = { target = ROOT type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_iraq_divisions
	icon = militarized_iraq

	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = SYR_greater_syria

	cost = 10

	prerequisite = { focus = SYR_greater_syria }

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = IRQ }
		NOT = { has_war_with = IRQ }
	}

	bypass = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = IRQ }
			IRQ = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_iraq_divisions"
		IRQ = {
			every_owned_state = {
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = KUR }
			KUR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRQ = { has_idea = sunni } }
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { NOT = { has_government = communism } } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { has_government = communism } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = nationalist
						size = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						NOT = { tag = IRQ }
					}
					remove_ideas = sunni
					add_ideas = shia
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRQ = { has_idea = shia } }
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { NOT = { has_government = nationalist } } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = nationalist
						size = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { has_government = nationalist } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						NOT = { tag = IRQ }
					}
					remove_ideas = shia
					add_ideas = sunni
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { IRQ = { country_event = SyriaFocus.65 } }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
		}
	}
}

	id = SYR_mop_up_iraq

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no

		NOT = { has_war_with = IRQ }
	}

		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = KUR }
			KUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_mop_up_iraq"
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRQ = { has_civil_war = no }
				country_exists = IRQ
			}
			set_temp_variable = { wargoal_on = IRQ }
			set_temp_variable = { wargoal_type = 2 }
			add_threat_from_wargoal_effect = yes
			create_wargoal = {
				target = IRQ
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRQ = { has_civil_war = yes }
			}
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = IRQ
				ROOT = {
					set_temp_variable = { wargoal_on = PREV }
					set_temp_variable = { wargoal_type = 2 }
					add_threat_from_wargoal_effect = yes
					create_wargoal = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = KUR
				KUR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { wargoal_on = KUR }
			set_temp_variable = { wargoal_type = 2 }
			add_threat_from_wargoal_effect = yes
			create_wargoal = {
				target = KUR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
		}
	}
}

	icon = tanks5

	mutually_exclusive = { focus = SYR_purchase_planes }

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_EQUIPMENT }

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_purchase_armoured_vehicles"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -2 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = democratic } #Western Syria will buy from France
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_chassis_2
					variant_name = "AMX-56 Leclerc"
					amount = 42
					producer = FRA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_flame_chassis
					amount = 50
					producer = FRA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_amphibious_chassis
					amount = 60
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = MBT_4		#Leclerc
					amount = 42
					producer = FRA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = IFV_3		#VIB
					amount = 50
					producer = FRA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = APC_5		#VAB Mk2
					amount = 60
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = communism }	#Emerging Syria will buy from Russia
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_meet_hamas
	icon = align_to_hamas

	x = -10
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = SYR_diplomatic_effort

	cost = 10

	prerequisite = { focus = SYR_affirm_claims_on_golan }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = SYR_meet_fatah }

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }

	available = {
		HAM = {
			NOT = { has_government = democratic }
			neutrality_neutral_social_in_power_or_coalition = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = syracc_negot
		}
		OR = {
			country_exists = HAM
			country_exists = PAL
		}
		OR = {
			HAM = { owns_state = 209 }
			PAL = { owns_state = 209 }
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_meet_hamas"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = HAM } }
			209 = { add_core_of = HAM }
			PAL = { release = HAM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = PAL
							is_claimed_by = PAL
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = PAL }
						add_core_of = HAM
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_claimed_by = PAL }
						add_claim_by = HAM
					}
				}
				HAM = { load_oob = HAM_2017 }
				ISR = {
					remove_state_claim = 209
					add_state_core = 209
				}
				PAL = {
					add_state_core = 209
				}
			}
			ISR = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
			PAL = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = HAM
			modifier = declaration_of_friendship
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = HAM
			modifier = declaration_of_friendship
		}
		HAM = {
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_arm_palestinians
	icon = align_to_hamas

	x = 23
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = SYR_diplomatic_effort

	cost = 10

	prerequisite = { focus = SYR_release_extremists }

	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }

	available = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = HAM
			country_exists = PAL
		}
		OR = {
			HAM = { owns_state = 209 }
			PAL = { owns_state = 209 }
		}
	}

	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = HAM }
		NOT = { PAL = { owns_state = 209 } }
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_arm_palestinians"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = HAM } }
			209 = { add_core_of = HAM }
			PAL = { release = HAM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = PAL
							is_claimed_by = PAL
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = PAL }
						add_core_of = HAM
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_claimed_by = PAL }
						add_claim_by = HAM
					}
				}
				HAM = { load_oob = HAM_2017 }
			}
			ISR = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
			PAL = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
		}
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_weapons_type
			amount = 1000
			target = HAM
		}
		HAM = {
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
		}
	}
}
